 When we reached Kanda's office, all the computers had been removed from there
 " unhone adaalat se apil kii ki kanda kii agrim jamaanat yachika khaarij kar di jaae, kyonki jaanch main sahyog ke liye notice di jane ke baavjood vah faraar ho gaye
 Luthra said that the investigation is still in the initial stage and it is necessary to interrogate Kanda from custody
 gauratlab he ki satr nyaayadhish kii adaalat ne kanda kii agrim jamaanat yachika chah agast ko yah kehete hue khaarij kar di thi ki unke khilaaf aarope chintajanak or sangeen hai or unki yachika main aisi koi khubi nahin he, jis aadhaar par jamaanat de di jaae
 Kanda has a case of abetment to suicide and bullying Geetika
 tippaniyan Kanda started his career as a small businessman and later started playing crores as a property dealer
 varsh 2007 main unhone emdlaar airlines kii shuruyaat kii thi
 He was elected to the Haryana Legislative Assembly as an independent candidate from Sirsa in the October 2009 elections
 unhone bhupendra singh hooda ke netritv vaali congress sarkaar ko samarthan dekar mantri pad hasil kii thi
 Additional Advocate General Siddharth Luthra, appearing for the Delhi Police, sought the custody of Kanda for questioning so that the conspiracy between Kanda and his company's senior officer Aruna Chadha could be discovered
 kanda kaa pratinidhitiv kar rahe varisht vakil keties tulsi ne dilli ucch nyaayalay se kaha ki suicide note ko 'purna satya' nahin mana ja saktaa
 Kanda wants anticipatory bail
 tulsi ne kaha, "suicide note gusse main likhe hue hote hai or koi aarope gusse main lagaae ja sakate hai
 "he said that the suicide notes written by Geetika cannot be considered complete
 gyaat ho ki vimaan paricharika rah chuki yuvati ne chaar-paanch agast kii raat apane ghar main pankhe main fanda daalkar faansee laga lee thi
 He wrote two suicide notes in which he blamed Kanda and Kanda's company senior officer Aruna Chadha for the suicide
 aruna giraftaar ho chuki he, jabaki kanda bhumigat ho gaye hai
 Tulsi said on behalf of Kanda, "maybe she likes me or i like her but that doesn't mean that i instigated her to commit suicide
 " unhone kaha ki geetika kii aatmahatya ke liye kanda ko jimmedaar tehraane ke liye kuch anya saboot jaruri hai
 Tulsi said, "the reasons given by the lower court while granting anticipatory bail are abuse of authority, showing more favor and exploitation towards Geetika, but these crimes do not come under the purview of abetment to suicide
" " unhone kaha ki geetika ek swabhimani ladki thi or vah aatmahatya ke liye nahin soch sakati thi
 Tulsi argued on behalf of Kanda, "even her mother and her brother did not know that she could commit suicide, then how could i know
" " At the same time, Siddharth Luthra opposed Kanda's anticipatory bail plea
 unhone kaha, "vah jaanch main sahyog nahin de rahe hai tathaa apane karyaalay se unhone laptop or commutaron sahit sabhi electronic saamaan hatwa liye hai
 As such, they should not be given anticipatory bail
 " The police lawyer told the court, "we are facing problems in the investigation
 jab ham kanda ke daftar main pahunche to vahaan se sabhi commuter hataae ja chuke the
 "he appealed to the court to dismiss Kanda's anticipatory bail plea, as he absconded despite being given notice to cooperate in the investigation
 luthra ne kaha ki jaanch abhi praarambhik charan main he or hiraasat main lekar kanda se poochtacha karnaa jaruri he
 Significantly, the court of Sessions Judge dismissed Kanda's anticipatory bail plea on August 6, saying that the charges against him were worrying and serious and there was no merit in his petition on the basis of which the bail was granted
 kanda ke khilaaf geetika ko aatmahatya ke liye uksaane or dhamkaane kaa maamla darj he
 The comments kanda ne chote vyavsaayee ke rup main apane kariyar kii shuruyaat kii thi or baad main property dealer banakar karodon main khilne lage

 aise ranneetik gunabhag ke chalate alpsankhyak vot bank saaf taur par bispi kii taraf ja saktaa he
 Not only this, the BJP is looking for OBC and MBC votes with stirring in its Mandal avatar
 vah sapa ke yadavon sahit obisi voton main send laga sakati he
 Finally, in 2014 in neighboring Bihar, the saffron party had breached Yadav's monopoly of RJD leader Lalu Prasad
 samaajawaadee party main agar koi netaa he jo sabhi dhadon ko saath lekar chal saktaa he or saath hi saath mahagathbandhan bhi khadaa kar saktaa he, to ve sirf mulaayam hai
 Despite all the gaiety and drama and disintegration, whether it is Shivpal or Amar Singh, Akhilesh or Ram Gopal, they all vouch for Netaji's leadership
 apane jivan ke sandhya kaal main vahi vah gond yaa saras hai jo party ko jodakar rakh sakati he
 He played a game with great prudence — he knew that the party was moving towards the break, especially with ticket distribution, when Shivpal's walkout was all the more likely, to go a soft way to keep him in the party, On the other hand, he also fully protected Akhilesh's interests
 itnaa hi nahin, agar akhilesh ke paas unke haq main javaani or karishma he, to shivpal ke paas party ko khadaa karne kaa 25 saal kaa tajurba he
 And even though Amar Singh and Ram Gopal do not mix eye to eye, both are excellent sportspersons of backstory politics and party work cannot work without both
 samaajawaadee party ke liye shaayad yah samajhane kaa vakt aa gaya he ki unke matbhed chaahe jo hon, saath milakar ve ab bhi ek vijeta team ban sakate hai
 The Supreme Court said that it would hear only on 'triple talaq' due to lack of time but in view of the Centre's emphasis, the issues of polygamy and 'nikah halala' are being kept open for future hearing, in the Supreme Court of the Center The Attorney General on behalf said that the central government is ready to enact a law on triple talaq
 unhone kaha ki is mudde par koi vaikum nahin he
 The Center said that the Supreme Court quashed three divorces, polygamy and halala
 bataa den ki supreme court ne kaha he ki teen talaak kii teenon farm yani talaak e biddat, talaak e hasana or talaak ke ahasan ko radd kar diya jaae ko kya hoga ? is par AG ne kaha sarkaar kanoon laane ko taiyaar he
 Earlier the AG said - talaak ke maamle main muslim samaaj main mahilaon ke adhikaar purushon kii tulana main kam
 Muslim women do not have equal rights as compared to women from other communities in the country
 videshon main um islamic deshon kii mahilaon ke mukaable bharat main muslim samudaay kii mahilaon ke adhikaar kam jahaan shaadi or talaak ko lekar rifarm ke taur par kanoon banaaya gaya
 The AG said in the Supreme Court - shaadi, talaak kaa dharm yaa dharmik pratha se koi lenaa dena nahin
 How can one's life be controlled
 court pavitra quran, guru granth sahib yaa gita kii vyakhya karne ke liye nahin he
 The Center told the Supreme Court - agar supreme court teen talaak, nikaah halaala or bahoovivaah ko radd kar detaa he to centre is par kanoon laane ko taiyaar
 There will be no vacuum on this issue AG ne ye daleel us vakt di jab court ne poocha ki agar court ise radd kar detaa he to muslim patiyon ke paas kya vikalp hoga ? The AG said in the Supreme Court - teen talaak samvidhan ke vipareet he
 It is against women's equality, gender equality and human rights
 koi bhi personal laa ho yaa pratha, use samvidhan kii kasuti se guzarana hoga
 Personal law should also be compared to right to equality, right to gender equality
 kisi bhi mahila ko duusare samudaay kii mahilaon ke samaan haq hona chahie
 AG said in court - ye minerti se juda samvedansheel mudda he isliye puraani sarkaar is par kanoon nahin laai - Personal laws taken from old texts should also be according to the constitution - teen talaak kii vajah se muslimon main aadhi aabaadi asahaay mahasoos kar rahi he - The citizens of a community in the country are not getting full fundamental rights
 AIMPLB kii ore se kapil sibbal ne supreme court main kaha
 
 
 - Women are discriminated against in every community - hindu lau ke mutabik pita par hota he ki wo beti ko jaaydaad main hissaa de yaa nahin - But in Muslim law, father has to give quarter to daughter
 - kya ye bhedbhaav nahin he - What do you want the daughter of Hindus to fight for divorce for years without getting any pie? sijeai jees khehar kii adhyakshata vaali paanch sadasyeey samvidhan peeth ne kaha, ‘‘hamaare paas jo simit samay he usamen teenon muddon ko nibataana sambhav nahin he
 We will keep them pending for the future
 ’’ adaalat ne yah baat tab kahi jab kendra sarkaar kii ore se pesh atarni general mukul rohtagi ne kaha ki do sadasyeey peeth ke jis aadesh ko samvidhan peeth ke samaksh pesh kiya gaya he usamen ‘teen talaak’ ke saath bahuvivaah or ‘nikaah halaala’ ke mudde bhi shaamil hai
 The Centre's view is significant in view of the court's comment that it will only deal with the issue of 'triple talaq' and that too when it is a fundamental issue for Islam
 peeth main nyaayamurti courian joseph, nyaayamurti aaref nariman, nyaayamurti yuyuu lalit or nyaayamurti abdul nazeer shaamil hai
 Rohatgi asked the Constitution Bench to make it clear that issues of polygamy and 'nikah halala' are still open and another bench will deal with it in future
 adaalat ne spasht kiya, ‘‘inhen bhavishya main nibataya jayega
 The Supreme Court is hearing petitions challenging the three divorces prevalent in Muslim society
 kendra ne aaj apni daleelein pesh kerani shuru kii he
 In the previous hearing, the Supreme Court raised many big questions
 court ne kaha tha ki teen talaak islam main shaadi khatm karne kaa sabase bura or avaanchhneeya tarika he
 Although triple divorce has been recognized as valid in various schools of Islam
 tripal talaak kya parampara he yaa shariat kaa hissaa he? Can one who is disgusted according to religion be valid under the law? What is a sin in the eyes of God, can it be taken in the Shari'a? Many people consider the death penalty to be a sin in the country, but it is valid by law
 agar bharat main tripal talaak vishisht he to duusare deshon ne kanoon banaakar tripal talaak ko khatm kar diya? (pehle din kii sunwaayee : teen talaak maamle par supreme court - agar yah dharm kaa maamla he to court isamen dakhal nahin degi)tippaniyan At the same time, former Law Minister and Congress leader Salman Khurshid, who is personally assisting the court, said that in my personal opinion triple divorce is a sin, but AIMPLB stands that triple divorce is abusive but still valid
 vahiin, ol india muslim mahila personal laa board ne bhi teen talaak ko gaiyrkanoonee qaraar diya he
 Explain that the Supreme Court has said what will happen if the three forms of triple talaq i
e
, talaq-e-biddat, talaq-e-lasana and abolition of divorce are canceled
 On this, the AG said that the government is ready to bring the law
 isse pehle AG ne kaha - In the case of divorce, women's rights in Muslim society are lower than men
 desh main anya samudaayon kii mahilaon kii tulana main muslim mahilaon ko samaan adhikaar nahin
 Women of Muslim community in India have less rights than women in Islamic countries abroad, where a law was enacted as a reform on marriage and divorce
 AG ne supreme court main kaha - Marriage, divorce have nothing to do with religion or religious practice
 kisi ke jivan ko kaise niyantrit kiya ja saktaa he
 The court is not meant to interpret the Holy Quran, the Guru Granth Sahib or the Gita
 centre ne supreme court se kaha - If the Supreme Court quits triple talaq, nikah halala and bahuivah, then the Center is ready to bring a law on it
 is mudde par koi vaikum nahin rahegaa The AG gave this argument at a time when the court asked that if the court quashed it, what option would Muslim husbands have? AG ne supreme court main kaha - The triple talaq is contrary to the constitution
 ye mahilaon ke samanta, langik samanta or maanavadhikaar ke khilaaf he
 Any personal person or practice, it has to go through the criteria of the constitution
 personal laa kii bhi samanta ke adhikaar, langik samanta ke adhikaar se tulana honi chahie
 Any woman should have the same rights as women of other communities
 AG ne court main kaha - This is a sensitive issue related to minorities, so the old government did not bring a law on it - puraane granthon se liye gaye personal laa bhi samvidhan ke mutabik hone chahine Half of the Muslim population is feeling helpless due to triple talaq
 - desh main ek samudaay ke nagarikon ko puure moulik adhikaar nahin mil rahe hai
 Kapil Sibal said in the Supreme Court on behalf of AIMPLB
 
 
 - har samudaay main mahilaon ke saath bhedbhaav hota he According to Hindu law, it is up to the father to give the daughter a share in the property or not
 - lekin muslim lau main pita ko chauthai hissaa beti ko dena hi hota he - Isn't this discrimination - aap kya chaahate hai ki hinduon main beti ko bina koi pai mili wo saalon tak talaak ke liye ladati rahen a five-member constitution bench headed by CJI JS Khehar said, "in the limited time we have, it is not possible to address all three issues
" ham unhen bhavishya ke liye lambit rakhenge
 The court said this when Attorney General Mukul Rohatgi, appearing on behalf of the Central Government, said that the order of the two-member bench which has been presented before the Constitution Bench includes 'triple talaq' with polygamy and 'nikah halala'
 Issues are also included
 kendra kii yah baat court kii is tippanee ke maddenjar ahm he ki vah sirf ‘teen talaak’ kaa mudda nibataayega or vah bhi tab jab yah islam ke liye buniyadi mudda hoga
 The bench consists of Justice Kurian Joseph, Justice RF Nariman, Justice UU Lalit and Justice Abdul Nazir
 rohtagi ne samvidhan peeth se yah saaf karne ke liye kaha ki bahuvivaah or ‘nikaah halaala’ ke mudde ab bhi khule hai or koi or peeth bhavishya main ise nibataayegi
 "these will be dealt with in future," the court clarified
 ’’ ucchtam nyaayalay muslim samaaj main vyaapt teen talaak ko chunauti dene vaali yachikaaon par sunwaayee kar rahi he
 The Center has started presenting its arguments today
 pichhali sunwaayee main supreme court ne kai bade sawaal uthaae the
 The court said that triple talaq is the worst and undesirable way to end marriage in Islam
 haalanki tripal talaak ko islam ke vibhinn skool of thats main ise vaid mana gaya he
 Is triple divorce a part of tradition or Sharia? kya jo dharm ke mutabik hi ghinauna he wo kanoon ke tahat vaid tehraaya ja saktaa he? jo ishwar kii najar main paap he kya use shariat main liya ja saktaa he? bahut saare log desh main maut kaa sajaa ko sin yani paap maanate hai lekin kanuunan ye vaid he
 If triple divorce is specific in India, then other countries have enacted laws and abolished triple divorce? (first day hearing: Supreme Court on triple talaq case - if it is a matter of religion then the court will not interfere in it) Comments vahiin nijee taur par court kii madad kar rahe purv kanoon mantri or congressi netaa salmaan khurshid ne kaha tha ki meri nijee raay main tripal talaak paap he, lekin AIMPLB kaa stand he ki tripal talaak ghinauna he lekin tab bhi vaid he

 vahiin, ol india muslim mahila personal laa board ne bhi teen talaak ko gaiyrkanoonee qaraar diya he
 The AG said in the Supreme Court - teen talaak samvidhan ke vipareet he
 It is against women's equality, gender equality and human rights
 koi bhi personal laa ho yaa pratha, use samvidhan kii kasuti se guzarana hoga
 Personal law should also be compared to right to equality, right to gender equality
 kisi bhi mahila ko duusare samudaay kii mahilaon ke samaan haq hona chahie
 AG said in court - ye minerti se juda samvedansheel mudda he isliye puraani sarkaar is par kanoon nahin laai - Personal laws taken from old texts should also be according to the constitution - teen talaak kii vajah se muslimon main aadhi aabaadi asahaay mahasoos kar rahi he - The citizens of a community in the country are not getting full fundamental rights
 AIMPLB kii ore se kapil sibbal ne supreme court main kaha
 
 
 - Women are discriminated against in every community - hindu lau ke mutabik pita par hota he ki wo beti ko jaaydaad main hissaa de yaa nahin - But in Muslim law, father has to give quarter to daughter
 - kya ye bhedbhaav nahin he - What do you want the daughter of Hindus to fight for divorce for years without getting any pie? sijeai jees khehar kii adhyakshata vaali paanch sadasyeey samvidhan peeth ne kaha, ‘‘hamaare paas jo simit samay he usamen teenon muddon ko nibataana sambhav nahin he
 We will keep them pending for the future
 ’’ adaalat ne yah baat tab kahi jab kendra sarkaar kii ore se pesh atarni general mukul rohtagi ne kaha ki do sadasyeey peeth ke jis aadesh ko samvidhan peeth ke samaksh pesh kiya gaya he usamen ‘teen talaak’ ke saath bahuvivaah or ‘nikaah halaala’ ke mudde bhi shaamil hai
 The Centre's view is significant in view of the court's comment that it will only deal with the issue of 'triple talaq' and that too when it is a fundamental issue for Islam
 peeth main nyaayamurti courian joseph, nyaayamurti aaref nariman, nyaayamurti yuyuu lalit or nyaayamurti abdul nazeer shaamil hai
 Rohatgi asked the Constitution Bench to make it clear that issues of polygamy and 'nikah halala' are still open and another bench will deal with it in future
 adaalat ne spasht kiya, ‘‘inhen bhavishya main nibataya jayega
 The Supreme Court is hearing petitions challenging the three divorces prevalent in Muslim society
 kendra ne aaj apni daleelein pesh kerani shuru kii he
 In the previous hearing, the Supreme Court raised many big questions
 court ne kaha tha ki teen talaak islam main shaadi khatm karne kaa sabase bura or avaanchhneeya tarika he
 Although triple divorce has been recognized as valid in various schools of Islam
 tripal talaak kya parampara he yaa shariat kaa hissaa he? Can one who is disgusted according to religion be valid under the law? What is a sin in the eyes of God, can it be taken in the Shari'a? Many people consider the death penalty to be a sin in the country, but it is valid by law
 agar bharat main tripal talaak vishisht he to duusare deshon ne kanoon banaakar tripal talaak ko khatm kar diya? (pehle din kii sunwaayee : teen talaak maamle par supreme court - agar yah dharm kaa maamla he to court isamen dakhal nahin degi)tippaniyan At the same time, former Law Minister and Congress leader Salman Khurshid, who is personally assisting the court, said that in my personal opinion triple divorce is a sin, but AIMPLB stands that triple divorce is abusive but still valid

 adaalat ne spasht kiya, ‘‘inhen bhavishya main nibataya jayega
 The Supreme Court is hearing petitions challenging the three divorces prevalent in Muslim society
 kendra ne aaj apni daleelein pesh kerani shuru kii he
 In the previous hearing, the Supreme Court raised many big questions
 court ne kaha tha ki teen talaak islam main shaadi khatm karne kaa sabase bura or avaanchhneeya tarika he

 agar bharat main tripal talaak vishisht he to duusare deshon ne kanoon banaakar tripal talaak ko khatm kar diya? (pehle din kii sunwaayee : teen talaak maamle par supreme court - agar yah dharm kaa maamla he to court isamen dakhal nahin degi)tippaniyan At the same time, former Law Minister and Congress leader Salman Khurshid, who is personally assisting the court, said that in my personal opinion triple divorce is a sin, but AIMPLB stands that triple divorce is abusive but still valid
 vahiin, ol india muslim mahila personal laa board ne bhi teen talaak ko gaiyrkanoonee qaraar diya he
 Kapil Sibal said in the Supreme Court on behalf of AIMPLB
 
 
 - har samudaay main mahilaon ke saath bhedbhaav hota he According to Hindu law, it is up to the father to give the daughter a share in the property or not
 - lekin muslim lau main pita ko chauthai hissaa beti ko dena hi hota he - Isn't this discrimination - aap kya chaahate hai ki hinduon main beti ko bina koi pai mili wo saalon tak talaak ke liye ladati rahen a five-member constitution bench headed by CJI JS Khehar said, "in the limited time we have, it is not possible to address all three issues
" ham unhen bhavishya ke liye lambit rakhenge
 The court said this when Attorney General Mukul Rohatgi, appearing on behalf of the Central Government, said that the order of the two-member bench which has been presented before the Constitution Bench includes 'triple talaq' with polygamy and 'nikah halala'
 Issues are also included
 kendra kii yah baat court kii is tippanee ke maddenjar ahm he ki vah sirf ‘teen talaak’ kaa mudda nibataayega or vah bhi tab jab yah islam ke liye buniyadi mudda hoga
 The bench consists of Justice Kurian Joseph, Justice RF Nariman, Justice UU Lalit and Justice Abdul Nazir
 rohtagi ne samvidhan peeth se yah saaf karne ke liye kaha ki bahuvivaah or ‘nikaah halaala’ ke mudde ab bhi khule hai or koi or peeth bhavishya main ise nibataayegi
 "these will be dealt with in future," the court clarified
 ’’ ucchtam nyaayalay muslim samaaj main vyaapt teen talaak ko chunauti dene vaali yachikaaon par sunwaayee kar rahi he
 The Center has started presenting its arguments today
 pichhali sunwaayee main supreme court ne kai bade sawaal uthaae the
 The court said that triple talaq is the worst and undesirable way to end marriage in Islam
 haalanki tripal talaak ko islam ke vibhinn skool of thats main ise vaid mana gaya he
 Is triple divorce a part of tradition or Sharia? kya jo dharm ke mutabik hi ghinauna he wo kanoon ke tahat vaid tehraaya ja saktaa he? jo ishwar kii najar main paap he kya use shariat main liya ja saktaa he? bahut saare log desh main maut kaa sajaa ko sin yani paap maanate hai lekin kanuunan ye vaid he
 If triple divorce is specific in India, then other countries have enacted laws and abolished triple divorce? (first day hearing: Supreme Court on triple talaq case - if it is a matter of religion then the court will not interfere in it) Comments vahiin nijee taur par court kii madad kar rahe purv kanoon mantri or congressi netaa salmaan khurshid ne kaha tha ki meri nijee raay main tripal talaak paap he, lekin AIMPLB kaa stand he ki tripal talaak ghinauna he lekin tab bhi vaid he
 At the same time, the All India Muslim Women Personal Law Board has also declared the triple talaq illegal
 sijeai jees khehar kii adhyakshata vaali paanch sadasyeey samvidhan peeth ne kaha, ‘‘hamaare paas jo simit samay he usamen teenon muddon ko nibataana sambhav nahin he
 We will keep them pending for the future

 Despite strict instructions from Uttar Pradesh Chief Minister Yogi Adityanath, about 120 IAS officers have not yet given details of their assets
 yogi sarkaar ne afasaron se apni chal-achal sampatti kaa byoraa dene ko kaha tha
 The officers were given a chance for the first 15 days
 iske baad phir avadhi badhaai gai, lekin mangalvaar ko byoraa dene kii avadhi samaapt hone ke baad bhi 120 iees afasaron ne apni chal sampatti or 30 ne apni achal sampatti kaa byoraa nahin diya
 After this, the Chief Secretary has now asked the principal secretaries of all the departments to provide details in this regard by May 3
 niyukti or carmik vibhaag ke ek varisht adhikari ne bataaya ki kuch logon ne mukhya sachiv ke paas bhi byoraa bheja hoga, to vahaan se aane main bhi ek-do din lag sakate hai, lekin 120 iees afasar apni chal sampatti nahin bataa sake hai
 He said that the officers submit the details of immovable property every year
 pehali baar unhen chal sampatti bataane ko kaha gaya tha
 Chief Secretary Rahul Bhatnagar issued a circular again on 20 April, expressing displeasure with the IAS officers who did not provide the details of the movable property
 unhone 25 april se pehle har haal main chal sampatti kaa vivaran uplabdh karaane ko kaha tha
 Even after this, the details could not be found
 ab mukhya sachiv rahul bhatnagar ne teen may ko sabhi pramukh sachivon kii ek baithak bulaai he
 Despite repeated instructions, officers who do not provide details may have to bear the brunt of this
 aise logon kii vaarshik pravishti roki ja sakati he
 Increment and promotion may also be affected
 desh ke share bazaaron main mangalvaar ko teji darj kii gai

 aaie jaanate hai is skim se judi 5 jaruri baaten
 
 1) kya he gold monetigeshan skim ?bhale hi gold monetigeshan skim kii charchaa chaaron ore ho lekin bahut kam logon ko hi isaki puri jaankaree or phaayde pataa hai
 Under this scheme you can deposit your gold in the bank, instead of which the bank will give you a fixed rate of interest
 yah phaayde kaa sauda isliye he kyonki jab aap loker lekar sona rakhte he to aapako bank ko paise chukaane padate hai lekin isamen ulte bank hi aapako paise degaa

 isamen gold-baar, sikke, gahane aadi shaamil honge
 Keep in mind that this will not include metal
 3) bank apane marji se tay karenge byaaj darasabhi vaanijya bainkon ko is skim ko shuru karne kii anumati he

 4) jamaa karne se pehle sone kii jaanchis skim main teen tareeke kii samyavadhi main sona jamaa kiya ja sakegaa
 Short term (1 to 3 years), medium term (5 to 7 years) and long term (12 to 15 years)

 Learn the last minute tips to crack an exam
 1
 First of all, repeat the topics you have prepared well
 agar aap kisi nae topic ko padhane ke bare main soch rahe hai to aisa nahin karen kyonki exam ke aakhir main kisi nae topic kii shuruyaat aapako kanphyus kar detii he
 2
 ek revijan time-teble banaaen, jisase aapako puri tarah pataa ho ki kya padhanaa rah gaya he or kya baaki bachaa he
 3
 saare fomule ek baad phir se doharaa len, aisa karne se aapako problem nahin hogi
 4
 exam ke aakhir main group study bhuulakar bhi nahin karen
 Doing this will give you tension
 5
 Test yourself by solving old papers and quashbanks
 6
 Do try the mock paper, it gives you an idea of how much time you have to spend in questions
 7
 After getting the paper on the exam day, read all the questions and then answer them
 paper padhane ke dauraan aapako pataa chal jayega ki koun-sa queshchan aapako pataa he or koun-sa nahin
 8
 khud ko shant rakhen
